<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;text-decoration:none underline;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:center;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;text-decoration:none underline;">Section 1 &ndash; Registrant&rsquo;s Business and Operations</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;margin-left:72pt;text-indent:-72pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">Item 1.01.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:36pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;On December 17, 2004, M-Wave, Inc. and Silicon Valley Bank entered into an Amendment to Loan Documents.&nbsp;&nbsp;The amendment revised M-Wave&rsquo;s credit limit under the Loan and Security Agreement (described below), by allowing M-Wave to include a portion of certain accounts receivable from customers who are not residents of the </em>United States<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;or </em>Canada<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;in its borrowing base. The foregoing summary description of the amendment is qualified in its entirety by reference to the terms of the amendment, which is filed as an exhibit hereto.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;text-indent:36pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:36pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;On June 28, 2004, M-Wave and Silicon Valley Bank entered into a Loan and Security Agreement, replacing a prior credit facility with a $4.5 million revolving credit facility that improved the terms, eligibility and pricing from the then-existing agreement with Silicon Valley Bank. The effective rate of interest under the June 28, 2004 agreement, including fees, is approximately 8%.&nbsp;&nbsp;M-Wave may borrow up to $4.5 million, or a lesser amount depending on M-Wave&rsquo;s borrowing base from time to time.&nbsp;&nbsp;The borrowing base consists of eligible receivables and eligible finished goods inventory, as further described in such agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;The agreement had previously been disclosed in M-Wave&rsquo;s filings.&nbsp;&nbsp;However, in connection with the preparation of this Current Re
port on Form 8-K to disclose and file the amendment described in Item 1.01(a) above, M-Wave discovered that the Loan and Security Agreement had not been filed previously.&nbsp;&nbsp;As a result, M-Wave is filing the Loan and Security Agreement herewith.&nbsp;&nbsp;The foregoing summary description of the agreement is qualified in its entirety by reference to the terms of the agreement, which is filed as an exhibit hereto.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">Item 9.01.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Financial Statements and Exhibits</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:36pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">(c)</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Exhibits</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:36pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:36pt;text-align:left;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:none underline;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Exhibit No.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Description</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:36pt;text-align:left;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:36pt;text-align:left;margin-left:108pt;text-indent:-72pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">10.1</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Amendment to Loan Documents, dated December 17, 2004, between M-Wave, Inc. and Silicon Valley Bank</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;margin-left:108pt;text-indent:-72pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">10.2</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Loan and Security Agreement, dated June 28, 2004, between M-Wave, Inc. and Silicon Valley Bank</em></em>

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;">(a)</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Definition of &ldquo;Eligible Domestic Accounts&rdquo;.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;&nbsp;The words &ldquo;Eligible Accounts&rdquo; in the definition of &ldquo;Eligible Accounts&rdquo; in Section 8 of the Loan Agreement are hereby changed to &ldquo;Eligible Domestic Accounts&rdquo; everywhere they appear in said definition.</em></em>

</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:36pt;margin-left:108pt;margin-right:36pt;text-indent:0pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&ldquo;&lsquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none underline;">Eligible Foreign Accounts</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&rsquo; means Accounts </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">and General Intangibles arising in the ordinary course of Borrower's business from the sale of goods or the rendition of services, or the non-exclusive licensing of Intellectual Property, which Silicon, in its good faith business judgment, shall deem eligible for borrowing, and which meet the Minimum Eligibility Requirements set forth abo
ve (as revised by Silicon from time to time), except that they are owing from an Account Debtor located outside the United States or Canada (a &lsquo;Foreign Account Debtor&rsquo;). Accounts owing from one Foreign Account Debtor will not be deemed </em><a name="OLE_LINK1"></a><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Eligible Foreign Accounts</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&nbsp;to the extent they exceed 25% of total Accounts outstanding.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addi</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&shy;tion, if more than 50% of the Accounts owing from a Foreign Account Debtor are outstanding for a period longer than their Eligibility Period (without regard to unapplied credits) or are otherwise not Eligible Foreign Accounts, then all Accounts owing from that Foreign Account Debtor will be de
emed ineligible for borrowing.&rdquo;</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:36pt;margin-left:108pt;margin-right:36pt;text-indent:0pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"></em>&nbsp;</em>

</p>

The Schedule to this Agreement (the &ldquo;Schedule&rdquo;) shall for all purposes be deemed to be a part of this Agreement, and the same is an integral part of this Agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;(Definitions of certain terms used in this Agreement are set forth in Section 8 below.) As set forth in the Amendment to Loan Documents of even date between Silicon and the Borrower, this Loan Agreement amends and restates in its entirety the Accounts Receivable Financing Agreement dated March 31, 2004 between Silicon and Borrower.</em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">1.</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;<em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">LOANS.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">1.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Loans. </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;Silicon will make loans to Borrower (the &ldquo;Loans&rdquo;) up to the amounts (the &ldquo;Credit Limit&rdquo;) shown on the Schedule, provided no Default or Event of Default has occurred and is continuing, and subject to deduction of Reserves for accrued interest and such other Reserves as Silicon deems proper from time to time in its good faith business judgment.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">1.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Interest.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;All Loans and all other monetary Obligations shall bear interest at the rate shown on the Schedule, except where expressly set forth to the contrary in this Agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;Interest shall be payable monthly, on the last day of the month.&nbsp;&nbsp;Interest shall be charged to Borrower&rsquo;s Deposit Accounts maintained with Silicon, if there are sufficient funds therein to pay the same, and if not, interest shall be charged to Borrower&rsquo;s loan account, and the same shall thereafter bear interest at the same rate as the other Loans. Regardless o
f the amount of Obligations that may be out</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;standing from time to time, Borrower shall pay Silicon minimum monthly interest during the term of this Agreement in the amount set forth on the Schedule (the &ldquo;Minimum Monthly Interest&rdquo;).</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">1.3&nbsp;&nbsp;Overadvances. </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;If at any time or for any reason the total of all outstanding Loans and all other monetary Obligations ex</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ceeds the Credit Limit (an &ldquo;Overadvance&rdquo;), Borrower shall immediately pay the amount of the excess to Silicon, with</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;out notice or demand.&nbsp;&nbsp;Without limiting Borrower's obliga</em><em style="font-style:
normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion to repay to Silicon the amount of any Overadvance, Borrower agrees to pay Silicon interest on the outstanding amount of any Overadvance, on demand, at the Default Rate.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">1.4&nbsp;&nbsp;Fees.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower shall pay Silicon the fees shown on the Schedule, which are in addition to all interest and other sums payable to Silicon and are not refundable.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">1.5 Loan Requests.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;To obtain a Loan, Borrower shall make a request to Silicon by facsimile or telephone. Loan requests received after 12:00 Noon will not be considered by Silicon until the next Business Day. Silicon may rely on any telephone request for a Loan given by a person whom Silicon believes is an authorized representative of Borrower, and Borrower will indemnify Silicon for any loss Silicon suffers as a result of that reliance.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">2.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;&nbsp;SECURITY INTEREST</em>. To secure the payment and per&shy;formance of all of the Obligations when due, Borrower hereby grants to Silicon a security interest in all of the following (collectively, the &ldquo;Collateral&rdquo;):&nbsp;&nbsp;all right, title and interest of Borrower in and to all of the following, whether now owned or hereafter arising or acquired and wherever located: all Accounts; all Inventory; all Equipment; all Deposit Accounts; all General Intangibles (including without limitation all Intellectual Property); all Investment Property; all Other Property; and any and all claims, rights and interests in any of the above, and all guaranties and security for any of the above, and all substitutions and replacements for, additions, accessions, attachments, accessories, and improvements to, and proceeds&nbsp;&nbsp;(in
cluding proceeds of any insurance policies, proceeds of proceeds and claims against third parties) of, any and all of the above, and all Borrower&rsquo;s books relating to any and all of the above.</em>
</p>

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">3.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;&nbsp;REPRESENTATIONS, WARRANTIES AND COVENANTS OF BORROWER.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">In order to induce Silicon to enter into this Agreement and to make Loans, Borrower represents and warrants to Silicon as follows, and Borrower covenants that the following representations will continue to be true, and that Borrower will at all times comply with all of the following covenants, throughout the term of this Agreement and until all Obligations have been paid and performed in full:</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">3.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Corporate Existence and Authority.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower is and will continue to be, duly organized, validly existing and in good standing under the laws of the jurisdiction of its incorporation.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower is and will con</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tinue to be qualified and licensed to do business in all ju</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;risdictions in which any failure to do so would result in 
a Material Adverse Change.&nbsp;&nbsp;The execution, delivery and performance by Borrower of this Agreement, and all other documents contemplated hereby (i) have been duly and validly authorized, (ii) are enforceable against Borrower in accordance with their terms (except as en</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;forcement may be limited by equitable principles and by bankruptcy, insolvency, reorganization, moratorium or similar laws relating to creditors' rights generally), and (iii) do not violate Borrower&rsquo;s articles or certificate of incorporation, or Borrower&rsquo;s by-laws, or any law or any&nbsp;&nbsp;material agreement or instru</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ment which is binding upon Borrower or its property, and (iv) do not constitute grounds for acceleration of any material indebtedness or obligation under any agreement or i
nstru</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ment which is binding upon Borrower or its property.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">3.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Name; Trade Names and Styles.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;The name of Borrower set forth in the heading to this Agreement is its correct name.&nbsp;&nbsp;Listed in the Representations are all prior names of Borrower and all of Borrower&rsquo;s present and prior trade names.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower shall give Silicon 30 days' prior written notice before changing its name or doing business under any other name.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower has complied, and will in the future comply, in all material respects, with all laws relating to the conduct of business under a fictitious business name, except where the 
failure to so comply would not reasonably be expected to result in a Material Adverse Change.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">3.3&nbsp;&nbsp;Place of Business; Location of Collateral. </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;The ad</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;dress set forth in the heading to this Agreement is Borrower's chief executive office.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, Borrower has places of business and Collateral is located only at the locations set forth in the Representations.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower will give Silicon at least 30 days prior written notice before opening any additional place of business, changing its chief execu</em><em style="font-style:normal;fo
nt-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tive office, or moving any of the Collateral to a location other than Borrower&rsquo;s Address or one of the locations set forth in the Representations, except that Borrower may maintain sales offices in the ordinary course of business at which not more than a total of $10,000 fair market value of Equipment is located.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">3.4&nbsp;&nbsp;Title to Collateral; Perfection; Permitted Liens.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower is now, and will at all times in the future be, the sole owner of all the Collateral, except for items of Equipment which are leased to Borrower.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Collateral now is and will remain free and clear of any and all liens, charges, security interests, encumbrances and adverse claims, except for Permitted Liens.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon now has, and will continue to have, a first-priority perfected and enforceable security in</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;terest in all of the Collateral, subject only to the Permitted Liens, and Borrower will at all times defend Silicon and the Collateral against all claims of others.&nbsp;&nbs
p;</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">(b)</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower has set forth in the Representations all of Borrower&rsquo;s Deposit Accounts, and Borrower will give Silicon five Business Days advance written notice before establishing any new Deposit Accounts and will cause the institution where any such new Deposit Account is maintained to execute and deliver to Silicon a control agreement in form sufficient to perfect Silicon&rsquo;s security interest in the Deposit Account and otherwise satisfactory to Silicon in its good faith business judgment.&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing herein limits any requirements which may be set forth in the Schedule as to where Deposit Ac
counts will be maintained.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">(c) In the event that Borrower shall at any time after the date hereof have any commercial tort claims against others, which it is asserting or intends to assert, and in which the potential recovery exceeds $100,000, Borrower shall promptly notify Silicon thereof in writing and provide Silicon with such information regarding the same as Silicon shall request (unless providing such information would waive the Borrower&rsquo;s attorney-client privilege).&nbsp;&nbsp;Such notification to Silicon shall constitute a grant of a security interest in the commercial tort claim and all proceeds thereof to Silicon, and Borrower shall execute and deliver all such documents and take all such actions as Silicon shall request in connection therewith.</em
></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">(d)</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;None of the Collateral now is or will be affixed to any real property in such a manner, or with such intent, as to become a fixture.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower is not and will not become a lessee under any real property lease pursuant to which the lessor may obtain any rights in any of the Collateral and no such lease now prohibits, restrains, impairs or will prohibit, restrain or im</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;pair Borrower's right to remove any Collateral from the leased premises.&nbsp;&nbsp;Whenever any Collateral is loca
ted upon premises in which any third party has an interest, Borrower shall, whenever requested by Silicon, use its best efforts to cause such third party to exe</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;cute and deliver to Silicon, in form acceptable to Silicon, such waivers and subordinations as Silicon shall specify in its good faith business judgment. Borrower will keep in full force and effect, and will comply with all material terms of, any lease of real property where any of the Collateral now or in the future may be located.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">

 therein stated.&nbsp;&nbsp;Between the last date covered by any such statement provided to Silicon and the date hereof, there has been no Material Adverse Change.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">3.8&nbsp;&nbsp;Tax Returns and Payments; Pension Contributions.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower has timely filed, and will timely file, all required tax returns and reports, and Borrower has timely paid, and will timely pay, all foreign, federal, state and local taxes, as</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;sessments, deposits and contributions now or in the future owed by Borrower.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower may, however, defer pay</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;fon
t-size:10pt;">&shy;ment of any contested taxes, provided that Borrower (i) in good faith contests Borrower's obligation to pay the taxes by appropriate proceedings promptly and diligently insti</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tuted and conducted, (ii) notifies Silicon in writing of the commencement of, and any material development in, the proceedings, and (iii) posts bonds or takes any other steps required to keep the contested taxes from becoming a lien upon any of the Collateral.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower is unaware of any claims or adjustments proposed for any of Borrower's prior tax years which could result in additional taxes becoming due and payable by Borrower.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower has paid, and shall continue to pay all amounts necessary to fund all pre</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;sent and future pension, profit sharing and deferred c
om</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;pensation plans in accordance with their terms, and Borrower has not and will not withdraw from participation in, permit partial or complete termination of, or permit the occurrence of any other event with respect to, any such plan which could reasonably be expected to result in any liability of Borrower, in</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;cluding any liability to the Pension Benefit Guaranty Corporation or its successors or any other governmental agency. </em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">3.9&nbsp;&nbsp;Compliance with Law.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower has, to the best of its knowledge, complied, and will comply, in all material respects, with all provisions of all foreign, federal, state and local laws and regulations applicable to Borrower, including, but not limited to, those relating to Borrower's ownership of real or personal prop</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;erty, the conduct and licensing of Borrower's business, and all environmental matters.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">3.10&nbsp;&nbsp;Litigation.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;There is no claim, suit, litigation, proceeding or investiga</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion pending or (to best of Borrower&rsquo;s knowledge) threat</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ened against or affecting Borrower in any court or before any governmental agency (or any basis therefor known to Borrower) which could reasonably be expected to result, either separately or in the ag
gregate, in any Material Adverse Change.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower will promptly inform Silicon in writing of any claim, proceeding, litigation or investigation in the future threatened or instituted against Borrower involving any single claim of </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">$50,000</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;or more, or involving </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">$100,000</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;or more in the aggregate.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">3.11&nbsp;&nbsp;Use of Proceeds.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;&nbsp;All proceeds of all Loans shall be used solely for lawful business purposes.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower is not purchasing or carrying any "margin stock" (as defined in Regulation U of the Board of Governors of the Federal Reserve System) and no part of the proceeds of any Loan will be used to purchase or carry any "margin stock" or to extend credit to others for the purpose of purchasing or carrying any "margin stock." </em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">4.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Representations Relating to Accounts. </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">Borrower represents and warrants to Silicon as follows:&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Account with respect to which Loans are requested by Borrower shall, on the date each Loan is requested and made, (i) represent an undisputed bona fide existing un</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;conditional obligation of the Account Debtor created by
 the sale, delivery, and acceptance of goods or the rendition of services, or the non-exclusive licensing of Intellectual Property, in the ordinary course of Borrower's business, and (ii) meet the Minimum Eligibility Requirements set forth in&nbsp;&nbsp;Section 8 below.</em></em>

y;ments and all of Borrower's books and records are and shall be genuine and in all respects what they purport to be.&nbsp;&nbsp;All sales and other transactions underlying or giving rise to each Account shall comply in all material respects with all applicable laws and governmental rules and regulations.&nbsp;&nbsp;To the best of Borrower&rsquo;s knowledge, all signatures and endorsements on all documents, instru</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ments, and agreements relating to all Accounts are and shall be genuine, and all such documents, instruments and agreements are and shall be legally enforceable in accor</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;dance with their terms.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">

atino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;vance or lend against a specific Account affect or limit Silicon's security interest and other rights therein. If requested by Silicon, Borrower shall furnish Silicon with copies (or, at Silicon's request, originals) of all contracts, orders, invoices, and other similar documents, and all shipping instructions, delivery receipts, bills of lading, and other evidence of delivery, for any goods the sale or disposition of which gave rise to such Accounts, and Borrower warrants the genuineness of all of the fore</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;going.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower shall also furnish to Silicon an aged ac</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;counts receivable trial balance as provided in the Schedule.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, Borrower shall deliver to Silicon, on its request, 
the originals of all instruments, chattel paper, security agreements, guarantees and other documents and property evidencing or securing any Accounts, in the same form as received, with all necessary indorsements, and copies of all credit memos.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">4.4&nbsp;&nbsp;Collection of Accounts. </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;Borrower shall have the right to collect all Accounts, unless and until a Default or an Event of Default has occurred and is continuing.&nbsp;&nbsp;Whether or not an Event of Default has occurred and is continuing, Borrower shall hold all payments on, and proceeds of, Accounts in trust for Silicon, and Borrower shall immediately deliver all such payments and proceeds to Silicon in their original form, duly endorsed, to be applied to the Obligations in such order as Silicon shall determine.&nbsp;&nbsp;All proceeds of Collateral shall be de</em><em s
tyle="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;posited by Borrower into a lockbox account, or such other "blocked account" as Silicon may specify, pursuant to a blocked account agreement in such form as Silicon may specify in its good faith business judgment. </em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">

ne; pro</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;vided that, if no Default or Event of Default has occurred and is continuing, Borrower shall not be obligated to remit to Silicon (i) the pro</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ceeds of the sale of worn out or obsolete Equipment dis</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;posed of by Borrower in good faith in an arm&rsquo;s length transaction for an aggregate purchase price of </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">$40,000</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;or less (for all such transactions in any fiscal year), or (ii) the proceeds of the Tax Refund&nbsp;&nbsp;or the pr
oceeds of the sale of the Real Property pursuant to Section 8(5) of the Schedule.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower agrees that it will not commingle proceeds of Collateral with any of Borrower's other funds or property, but will hold such proceeds separate and apart from such other funds and property and in an express trust for Silicon.&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Section limits the restrictions on disposi</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion of Collateral set forth elsewhere in this Agreement.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:13.5pt;">

10pt;">&shy;ported to Silicon on the regular reports provided to Silicon; (ii) no Default or Event of Default has occurred and is con</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tinuing; and (iii) taking into account all such discounts, set</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tlements and forgiveness, the total outstanding Loans will not exceed the Credit Limit.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">

he occurrence and during the continuance of any Event of Default, Borrower shall hold the returned Inventory in trust for Silicon, and&nbsp;immediately notify Silicon of the return of the Inventory.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></em>

;&nbsp;Nothing herein shall, however, relieve Silicon from liability for its own gross negligence or willful misconduct.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">5.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Insurance.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower shall, at all times, insure all of the tangible personal property Collateral and carry such other business insurance, with insurers reasonably accept</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;able to Silicon, in such form and amounts as Silicon may reasonably require and that are customary and in accordance with standard practices for Borrower&rsquo;s industry and locations, and Borrower shall provide evidence of such insurance to Silicon.&nbsp;&nbsp;All such insurance pol
icies shall name Silicon as an additional loss payee, and shall contain a lenders loss payee en</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;dorsement in form reasonably acceptable to Silicon.&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon receipt of the proceeds of any such insurance with respect to tangible personal property Collateral (and not real property), Silicon shall apply such proceeds in reduction of the Obligations as Silicon shall determine in its good faith business judgment, except that, provided no Default or Event of Default has occurred and is continuing, Silicon shall release to Borrower insurance proceeds with respect to Equipment totaling less than $100,000, which shall be utilized by Borrower for the re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;placement of the Equipment with respect to which the in</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times 
New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;surance proceeds were paid.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon may require reason</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;able assurance that the insurance proceeds so released will be so used.&nbsp;&nbsp;If Borrower fails to provide or pay for any in</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;surance, Silicon may, but is not obligated to, obtain the same at Borrower's expense.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower shall promptly de</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;liver to Silicon copies of all material reports made to insurance companies.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">5.3&nbsp;&nbsp;Reports.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower, at its expense, shall provide Silicon with the written reports set forth in the Schedule, and such other written reports with respect to Borrower (including budgets, sales projections, operating plans and other financial documentation), as Silicon shall from time to time specify in its good faith business judgment.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">5.4&nbsp;&nbsp;Access to Collateral, Books and Records.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;At rea</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;sonable times, and on one Business Day&rsquo;s notice, Silicon, or its agents, shall have the right to inspect the Collateral, and the right to audit and copy Borrower's books and records.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon shall take reasonable steps to keep confi</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;dential all information obtained in any
 such inspection or audit, but Silicon shall have the right to disclose any such information to its auditors, regulatory agencies, and attor</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;neys, and pursuant to any subpoena or other legal process.&nbsp;&nbsp;The foregoing inspections and audits shall be at Borrower&rsquo;s expense and the charge therefor shall be $750 per person per day (or such higher amount as shall repre</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;sent Silicon&rsquo;s then current standard charge for the same), plus reasonable out-of-pocket expenses. In the event Borrower and Silicon schedule an audit more than 10 days in advance, and Borrower seeks to reschedules the audit with less than 10 days written notice to Silicon, then (without limiting any of Silicon&rsquo;s rights or remedies), Borrower shall reimburse Silicon for all out-of-pocket expe
nses incurred by Silicon as a result of the cancellation.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">5.5&nbsp;&nbsp;Negative Covenants.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as may be permitted in the Schedule, Borrower shall not, without Silicon's prior written consent (which shall be a matter of its good faith business judgment, and which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld), do any of the following:&nbsp;&nbsp;(i) merge or con</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;solidate with another corporation or entity, except that the Sub may be merged into M-Wave, Inc., as provided in Section 8(6) of the Schedule ; (ii) acquire any 
assets, except in the ordinary course of business; (iii) enter into any other transaction outside the ordinary course of business; (iv) sell or transfer any Collateral, except for the sale of finished Inventory in the ordinary course of Borrower's business, and except for the sale of obsolete or unneeded Equipment in the ordinary course of business; (v) store any Inventory or other Collateral with any </em><a name="OLE_LINK2"></a><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">ware</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;houseman or other third party</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">, except for Inventory so stored in the ordinary course of business and as to which the ware</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;hou
seman or other third party has executed and delivered to Silicon a waiver and agreement in such form as Silicon shall specify; (vi) sell any Eligible Inventory on a sale-or-return, guaranteed sale, consignment, or other con</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tingent basis (but Borrower may sell Inventory which is not Eligible Inventory on a sale-or-return, guaranteed sale, consignment, or other con</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tingent basis, if Borrower gives prior written notice thereof to Silicon and provides such information concerning the same as Silicon shall request); (vii) make any loans of any money or other assets; (viii) incur any debts, outside the ordinary course of business, which would result in a Material Adverse Change; (ix) guarantee or otherwise become liable with respect to the obligations of another party or entity; (x)
 pay or declare any dividends on Borrower's stock (except for dividends payable solely in stock of Borrower); (xi) redeem, retire, purchase or otherwise acquire, directly or indirectly, any of Borrower's stock or other equity securities, except solely for stock or other equity securities of the Borrower; (xii) make any change in Borrower's capital structure which would result in a Material Adverse Change; or (xiii) engage, directly or indirectly, in any business other than the businesses currently engaged in by Borrower or reasonably related thereto; or (xiv) dissolve or elect to dissolve.&nbsp;&nbsp;Transactions permitted by the foregoing provisions of this Section are only permitted if no Default or Event of Default would occur as a result of such transac</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">5.6&nbsp;&nbsp;Litigation Cooperation.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Should any third-party suit or proceeding be instituted by or against Silicon with re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;spect to any Collateral or relating to Borrower, Borrower shall, without expense to Silicon, make available Borrower and its officers, employees and agents and Borrower's books and records, to the extent that Silicon may deem them reasonably necessary in order to prosecute or defend any such suit or proceeding.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">5.7&nbsp;&nbsp;Further Assurances.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower agrees, at its ex</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;pense, on request by Silicon, to execute all documents and take all actions, as Silicon, may, in its good faith business judgment, deem neces</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;sary or useful in order to perfect and maintain Silicon's perfected first-priority security interest in the Collateral (subject to Permitted Liens), and in order to fully consummate the transactions contemplated by this Agreement.</em></em>

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">6.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Maturity Date.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;This Agreement shall continue in effect until the maturity date set forth on the Schedule (the "Maturity Date&rdquo;), subject to Section 6.3 below.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">6.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Early Termination.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;This Agreement may be termi</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;nated prior to the Maturity Date as follows:&nbsp;&nbsp;(i) by Borrower, effective three Business Days after written notice of termination is given to Silicon; or (ii) by Silicon at any time after the occurrence and during the continuance of an Event of Default, without notice, effective immediately.&nbsp;&nbsp;If this Agreement is termi</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palati
no;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;nated by Borrower or by Silicon under this Section 6.2, Borrower shall pay to Silicon a termination fee in an amount equal to one-half of one percent (0.5%) of the Maximum Credit Limit, provided that no termination fee shall be charged if the credit facility hereunder is replaced with a new facility from another division of Silicon Valley Bank, or if this Agreement is terminated by Silicon.&nbsp;&nbsp;The termination fee shall be due and payable on the effective date of termination and thereafter shall bear interest at a rate equal to the highest rate appli</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;cable to any of the Obligations.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">6.3&nbsp;&nbsp;Payment of Obligations.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;&nbsp;On the Maturity Date or on any earlier effective date of termination, Borrower shall pay and perform in full all Obligations, whether evidenced by installment notes or otherwise, and whether or not all or any part of such Obligations are otherwise then due and payable.&nbsp;&nbsp;Without limiting the generality of the foregoing, if on the Maturity Date,&nbsp;&nbsp;or on any earlier effective date of termination, there are any outstanding Letters of Credit is</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;sued by Silicon or issued by another institution based upon an application, guarantee, indemnity or similar agreement on the part of Silicon, then on such date Borrower 
shall provide to Silicon cash collateral in an amount equal to 105% of the face amount of all such Letters of Credit plus all interest, fees and cost due or to become due in connection there</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;with (as estimated by Silicon in its good faith business judgment), to secure all of the Obligations relating to said Letters of Credit, pursuant to Silicon&rsquo;s then standard form cash pledge agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding any termination of this Agreement, all of Silicon's security interests in all of the Collateral and all of the terms and provisions of this Agreement shall continue in full force and effect until all Obligations have been paid and performed in full; pro</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;vided that Silicon may, in its sole discretion, refuse to make any further Loans after termination.&nbsp;&nbsp;No termination shall in any way affect or impair any right or remedy of Silicon, nor shall any su
ch termination re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;lieve Borrower of any Obligation to Silicon, until all of the Obligations have been paid and performed in full.&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon payment and performance in full of all the Obligations and termination of this Agreement, Silicon shall promptly terminate its financing statements with respect to the Borrower and de</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;liver to Borrower such other documents as may be required to fully terminate Silicon's security interests.</em></em>
