:10pt;">&shy;tation, statement, report or certificate made or delivered to Silicon by Borrower or any of Borrower's officers, em</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ployees or agents, now or in the future, shall be untrue or misleading in a material respect when made or deemed to be made; or (b) Borrower shall fail to pay when due any Loan or any interest thereon or any other monetary Obligation, within three Business Days after the date due; or (c) the total Loans and other Obligations outstanding at any time shall exceed the Credit Limit; or (d) Borrower shall fail to comply with any of the financial covenants set forth in the Schedule, or shall fail to perform any other non-monetary Obligation which by its nature cannot be cured, or shall fail to permit Silicon to conduct an inspection or audit as specified in Section 5.4 hereof; or (e) Borrower shall fail to per</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-fam
ily:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;form any other non-monetary Obligation, which failure is not cured within five Business Days after the date due; or (f) any levy, assessment, attachment, seizure, lien or encum</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;brance (other than a Permitted Lien) is made on all or any part of the Collateral which is not cured within 10 days af</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ter the occurrence of the same; or (g) any default or event of default occurs under any obligation secured by a Permitted Lien, which is not cured within any applicable cure period or waived in writing by the holder of the Permitted Lien; or (h) Borrower breaches any material contract or obligation, which has resulted or may reasonably be ex</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#00
0000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;pected to result in a Material Adverse Change; or (i) Dissolution, termina</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion of existence, insolvency or business failure of Borrower; or appointment of a receiver, trustee or custo</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;dian, for all or any part of the property of, assignment for the benefit of creditors by, or the commencement of any proceeding by Borrower under any reorganization, bankruptcy, insolvency, arrangement, readjustment of debt, dissolution or liquidation law or statute of any juris</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;diction, now or in the future in effect; or (j) the com</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;men
cement of any proceeding against Borrower or any guarantor of any of the Obligations under any reorganiza</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion, bankruptcy, insolvency, arrangement, readjustment of debt, dissolution or liquidation law or statute of any juris</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;diction, now or in the future in effect, which is not cured by the dismissal thereof within 30 days after the date commenced; or (k) revocation or termination of, or limita</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion or denial of liability upon, any guaranty of the Obligations or any attempt to do any of the foregoing, or commencement of proceedings by any guarantor of any of the Obligations under any bankruptcy or insolvency law; or (l) revocation or termination of, or limitat
ion or denial of liability upon, any pledge of any certificate of deposit, securities or other property or asset of any kind pledged by any third party to secure any or all of the Obligations, or any attempt to do any of the foregoing, or commencement of proceedings by or against any such third party under any bankruptcy or insolvency law; or (m) Borrower makes any payment on account of any indebtedness or obligation which has been subordinated to the Obligations other than as permitted in the applicable subordination agreement, or if any Person who has subordinated such indebtedness or obligations terminates or in any way limits his subordina</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion agreement; or (n) there shall be a change in the record or beneficial ownership of an aggregate of more than 20% of the outstanding shares of voting stock of Borrower, in one or more transactions, compared to the ownership of outstand</em><em style
="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ing shares of voting stock of Borrower in effect on the date hereof, without the prior written consent of Silicon; or (o) Borrower shall generally not pay its debts as they become due, or Borrower shall conceal, remove or transfer any part of its property, with intent to hinder, delay or defraud its creditors, or make or suffer any transfer of any of its prop</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;erty which may be fraudulent under any bankruptcy, fraudulent conveyance or similar law; or (p) a Material Adverse Change shall occur.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon may cease making any Loans hereunder during any of the above cure periods, and thereafter if an Event of Default has occurred and is continuing.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">7.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Remedies.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon the occurrence and during the continuance of any Event of Default, and at any time thereafter, Silicon, at its option, and without notice or demand of any kind (all of which are hereby expressly waived by Borrower), may do any one or more of the following: (a) Cease making Loans or other</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;wise extending credit to Borrower under this Agreement or any other Loan Document; (b) Accelerate and de</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:P
alatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;clare all or any part of the Obligations to be immediately due, payable, and performable, notwithstanding any de</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ferred or installment payments allowed by any instrument evidencing or relating to any Obligation; (c) Take posses</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;sion of any or all of the Collateral wherever it may be found, and for that purpose Borrower hereby authorizes Silicon without judicial process to enter onto any of Borrower's premises without interference to search for, take possession of, keep, store, or remove any of the Collateral, and remain on the premises or cause a custo</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;dian to remain on the premises in excl
usive control thereof, without charge for so long as Silicon deems it necessary, in its good faith business judgment, in order to complete the enforcement of its rights under this Agreement or any other agreement; provided, however, that should Silicon seek to take posses</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;sion of any of the Collateral by court process, Borrower hereby irrevocably waives: (i) any bond and any surety or security relating thereto required by any statute, court rule or otherwise as an incident to such possession; (ii) any demand for possession prior to the commencement of any suit or action to recover possession thereof; and (iii) any requirement that Silicon retain possession of, and not dis</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;pose of, any such Collateral until after trial or final judg</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:
Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ment; (d) Require Borrower to assemble any or all of the Collateral and make it available to Silicon at places desig</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;nated by Silicon which are reasonably convenient to Silicon and Borrower, and to remove the Collateral to such locations as Silicon may deem advisable; (e) Complete the processing, manufacturing or repair of any Collateral prior to a disposition thereof and, for such purpose and for the purpose of removal, Silicon shall have the right to use Borrower's premises, vehicles, hoists, lifts, cranes, and other Equip</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ment and all other property without charge; (f) Sell, lease or otherwise dispose of any of the Collateral, in its condi</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-fami
ly:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion at the time Silicon obtains possession of it or after further manufacturing, processing or repair, at one or more public and/or private sales, in lots or in bulk, for cash, ex</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;change or other property, or on credit, and to adjourn any such sale from time to time without notice other than oral announcement at the time scheduled for sale.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon shall have the right to conduct such disposition on Borrower's premises without charge (subject to the terms of any lease with respect to the premises), for such time or times as Silicon deems reasonable, or on Silicon's premises, or elsewhere and the Collateral need not be located at the place of dis</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;position.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon may directly or through any affiliate
d company purchase or lease any Collateral at any such pub</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;lic disposition, and if permissible under applicable law, at any private disposition.&nbsp;&nbsp;Any sale or other disposition of Collateral shall not relieve Borrower of any liability Borrower may have if any Collateral is defective as to title or physical condition or otherwise at the time of sale; (g) Demand payment of, and collect any Accounts and General Intangibles comprising Collateral and, in connec</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion therewith, Borrower irrevocably authorizes Silicon to endorse or sign Borrower's name on all collections, receipts, instruments and other documents, to take posses</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;sion of and open mail addresse
d to Borrower and remove therefrom payments made with respect to any item of the Collateral or proceeds thereof, and, in Silicon's good faith business judgment, to grant extensions of time to pay, compromise claims and settle Accounts and the like for less than face value; (h) Offset against any sums in any of Borrower&rsquo;s general, special or other Deposit Accounts with Silicon against any or all of the Obligations; and (i) Demand and receive possession of any of Borrower's federal and state income tax returns and the books and records utilized in the preparation thereof or re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ferring thereto.&nbsp;&nbsp;All reasonable attorneys' fees, expenses, costs, liabilities and obligations incurred by Silicon with respect to the foregoing shall be added to and become part of the Obligations, shall be due on demand, and shall bear interest at a rate equal to the highest interest rate applicable to a
ny of the Obligations.&nbsp;&nbsp;Without limiting any of Silicon's rights and remedies, from and after the occurrence and during the continuance of any Event of Default, the interest rate applicable to the Obligations shall be increased by an additional four percent per annum over the interest rate otherwise applicable (the &ldquo;Default Rate&rdquo;).</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">7.3&nbsp;&nbsp;Standards for Determining Commercial Reasonableness.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower and Silicon agree that a sale or other disposition (collectively, &ldquo;sale&rdquo;) of any Collateral which complies with the following standards will conclu</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;sively be deemed to be commercially reasonable:&nbsp;&nbsp;(i) Notice of the sale is given to Borrower at least ten days prior to the sale, and, in the case of a public sale, notice of the sale is published at least five days before 
the sale in a newspaper of general circulation in the county where the sale is to be conducted; (ii) Notice of the sale describes the collateral in general, non-specific terms; (iii) The sale is conducted at a place designated by Silicon, with or without the Collateral being present; (iv) The sale commences at any time between 8:00 a.m. and 6:00 p.m;&nbsp;&nbsp;(v) Payment of the purchase price in cash or by cashier&rsquo;s check or wire transfer is required; (vi) With respect to any sale of any of the Collateral, Silicon may (but is not obligated to) direct any prospective purchaser to ascertain directly from Borrower any and all information concerning the same.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon shall be free to employ other methods of noticing and selling the Collateral, in its discretion, if they are commercially reasonable.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">7.4&nbsp;&nbsp;Power of Attorney.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon the occurrence and during the continuance of any Event of Default, without limiting Silicon&rsquo;s other rights and remedies, Borrower grants to Silicon an irrevocable power of attorney coupled with an interest, authorizing and permitting Silicon (acting through any of its employees, attorneys or agents) at any time, at its option, but without obligation, with or without notice to Borrower, and at Borrower's expense, to do any or all of the following, in Borrower's name or otherwise, but Silicon agrees that if it exercises any right hereunder
, it will do so in good faith and in a commercially reasonable manner:&nbsp;&nbsp;(a) Execute on behalf of Borrower any docu</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ments that Silicon may, in its good faith business judgment, deem advis</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;able in order to perfect and maintain Silicon's security in</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;terest in the Collateral, or in order to exercise a right of Borrower or Silicon, or in order to fully consummate all the transactions contemplated under this Agreement, and all other Loan Documents; (b) Execute on behalf of Borrower, any invoices relating to any Account, any draft against any Account Debtor and any notice to any Account Debtor, any proof of claim in bankruptcy, any Notice of Lien, claim of m
echanic's, materialman's or other lien, or assignment or satisfaction of mechanic's, materialman's or other lien; (c) Take control in any manner of any cash or non-cash items of payment or proceeds of Collateral; en</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;dorse the name of Borrower upon any instruments, or doc</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;uments, evidence of payment or Collateral that may come into Silicon's possession; (d) Endorse all checks and other forms of remittances received by Silicon; (e) Pay, contest or settle any lien, charge, encumbrance, security interest and adverse claim in or to any of the Collateral, or any judgment based thereon, or otherwise take any action to terminate or discharge the same; (f) Grant extensions of time to pay, compromise claims and settle Accounts and General Intangibles for less than face value and execute
 all releases and other documents in connection therewith; (g) Pay any sums required on account of Borrower's taxes or to secure the release of any liens therefor, or both; (h) Settle and adjust, and give releases of, any insurance claim that relates to any of the Collateral and obtain payment therefor; (i) Instruct any third party having custody or con</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;trol of any books or records belonging to, or relating to, Borrower to give Silicon the same rights of access and other rights with respect thereto as Silicon has under this Agreement; and (j) Take any action or pay any sum re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;quired of Borrower pursuant to this Agreement and any other Loan Documents.&nbsp;&nbsp;Any and all reasonable sums paid and any and all reasonable costs, expenses, lia</em><em style="font-style:normal;fon
t-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;bilities, obligations and attorneys' fees incurred by Silicon with respect to the foregoing shall be added to and become part of the Obligations, shall be payable on demand, and shall bear interest at a rate equal to the highest interest rate applicable to any of the Obligations.&nbsp;&nbsp;In no event shall Silicon's rights under the foregoing power of attorney or any of Silicon's other rights under this Agreement be deemed to indicate that Silicon is in control of the busi</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ness, management or properties of Borrower.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">7.5&nbsp;&nbsp;Application of Proceeds.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;All proceeds realized as the result of any sale of the Collateral shall be applied by Silicon first to the reasonable costs, expenses, liabilities, obligations and attorneys' fees incurred by Silicon in the exercise of its rights under this Agreement, second to the interest due upon any of the Obligations, and third to the principal of the Obligations, in such order as Silicon shall determine in its sole discretion.&nbsp;&nbsp;Any surplus shall be paid to Borrower or other persons legally entitled thereto; Borrower shall remain liable to Sili
con for any deficiency.&nbsp;&nbsp;If Silicon, in its good faith business judgment, directly or indirectly en</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ters into a deferred payment or other credit transaction with any purchaser at any sale of Collateral, Silicon shall have the option, exercisable at any time, in its good faith business judgment, of either reducing the Obligations by the principal amount of purchase price or deferring the reduction of the Obligations until the actual receipt by Silicon of the cash therefor.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">7.6&nbsp;&nbsp;Remedies Cumulative.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to the rights and remedies set forth in this Agreement, Silicon shall have all the other rights and remedies accorded a secured party un</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;der the California Uniform Commercial Code and under all other applicable laws, and under any other instrument or agreement now or in the future entered into between Silicon and Borrower, and all of such rights and remedies are cumulative and none is exclusive.&nbsp;&nbsp;Exercise or partial exercise by Silicon of one or more of its rights or remedies shall not be deemed an election, nor bar Silicon from sub</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;sequen
t exercise or partial exercise of any other rights or remedies.&nbsp;&nbsp;The failure or delay of Silicon to exercise any rights or remedies shall not operate as a waiver thereof, but all rights and remedies shall continue in full force and ef</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&shy;fect until all of the Obligations have been fully paid and performed.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">DEFINITIONS.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;&nbsp;As used in this Agreement, the following terms have the following meanings:</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Account Debtor</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means the obligor on an Account.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Accounts</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means all present and future &ldquo;accounts&rdquo; as defined in the California Uniform Commercial Code in effect on the date hereof with such additions to such term as may hereafter be made, and includes without limitation all accounts receivable and other sums owing to Borrower.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Affiliate</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means, with respect to any Person, a relative, partner, shareholder, director, officer, or employee of such Person, or any parent or subsidiary of such Person, or any Person controlling, controlled by or under common control with such Person.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">"</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Business Day</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">" means a day on which Silicon is open for business.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Code</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means the Uniform Commercial Code as adopted and in effect in the State of </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">California</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;from time to time. </em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Collateral</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; has the meaning set forth in Section 2 above.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">continuing</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; and &ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">during the continuance of</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; when used with reference to a Default or Event of Default means that the Default or Event of Default has occurred and has not been either waived in writing by Si
licon or cured within any applicable cure period.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Default</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means any event which with notice or passage of time or both, would constitute an Event of Default.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Default Rate</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; has the meaning set forth in Section 7.2 above.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Deposit Accounts</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means all present and future &ldquo;deposit accounts&rdquo; as defined in the California Uniform Commercial Code in effect on the date hereof with such additions to such term as may hereafter be made, and includes without limitation&nbsp;&nbsp;all general and special bank accounts, demand accounts, checking accounts, savings accounts and certificates of deposit.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">"</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Eligible Inventory</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">" means Inventory which Silicon, in its good faith business judgment, deems eligible for borrowing.&nbsp;&nbsp;Without limiting the fact that the determination of which Inventory is eligible for borrowing is a matter of Silicon&rsquo;s good faith business judgment, the following are the minimum requirements for Inventory to be Eligible Inventory:&nbsp;&nbsp;the Inventory must (i)&nbsp;consist of raw materials or fin</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palat
ino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ished goods, in good, new and salable condition, not be perishable, not be obsolete or unmerchantable, and not be comprised of work in process, packaging materials or supplies; (ii)&nbsp;meet all applicable governmen</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tal standards; (iii) have been manufactured in compliance with the Fair Labor Standards Act; (iv)&nbsp;conform in all re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;spects to the warranties and representations set forth in this Agreement; (v)&nbsp;be at all times subject to Silicon's duly per</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;fected, first priority security interest; and (vi) be in Borrower&rsquo;s exclusive control, and be situated at Borrower&rsquo;s Addre
ss or at one of the locations set forth in the Representations, provided that Inventory located at customers in the ordinary course of business may be Eligible Inventory, if (A) the Inventory is not located at more than a total of three locations for all customers, and (B) the customers at whose location the Inventory is located execute and deliver to Silicon waivers and agreements in such form as Silicon shall specify, and (C) Borrower provides reports as to such Inventory with such frequency and in such form as Silicon shall specify and separately identifies such Inventory on the Inventory reports provided for in Section 6 of the Schedule.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Eligible Accounts</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means Accounts and General Intangibles arising in the ordinary course of Borrower's business from the sale of goods or the rendition of services, or the non-exclusive licensing of Intellectual Property, which Silicon, in its good faith business judgment, shall deem eligible for borrowing.&nbsp;&nbsp;Without limiting the fact that the determina</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;
">&shy;tion of which Accounts are eligible for borrowing is a matter of Silicon&rsquo;s good faith business judgment, the following (the &ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Minimum Eligibility Requirements</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo;) are the minimum requirements for a Account to be an Eligible Account:&nbsp;&nbsp;(i) the Account must not be outstanding for more than 90 days from its invoice date (the &ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Eligibility Period</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo;), (ii) the Account must not represent progress billings, or be due under a fulfillment or requirements contract with 
the Account Debtor, (iii) the Account must not be subject to any contingencies (including Accounts arising from sales on consignment, guaranteed sale or other terms pursuant to which payment by the Account Debtor may be condi</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tional), (iv) the Account must not be owing from an Account Debtor with whom Borrower has any dispute (whether or not relating to the particular Account), (v) the Account must not be owing from an Affiliate of Borrower, (vi) the Account must not be owing from an Account Debtor which is subject to any insolvency or bankruptcy proceeding, or whose financial condition is not acceptable to Silicon, or which fails or goes out of a mate</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;rial portion of its business, (vii) the Account must not be owing from the United States or any department, agency or instrume
ntality thereof (unless there has been compliance, to Silicon&rsquo;s satisfaction, with the United States Assignment of Claims Act), (viii) the Account must not be owing from an Account Debtor located outside the United States or Canada (unless pre-approved by Silicon in its discretion in writing, or backed by a letter of credit sat</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;isfactory to Silicon, or FCIA insured satisfactory to Silicon),&nbsp;&nbsp;(ix) the Account must not be owing from an Account Debtor to whom Borrower is or may be liable for goods purchased from such Account Debtor or otherwise (</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">but, in such case, the Account will be deemed not eligible only to the extent of any amounts owed by Borrower to such Account Debtor)</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000
000;font-size:10pt;">. Accounts owing from one Account Debtor will not be deemed Eligible Accounts to the extent they exceed 25% of the total Accounts outstanding, provided that, in the case of Celistica Corporation, such percentage shall be 40%.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addi</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion, if more than 50% of the Accounts owing from an Account Debtor are outstanding for a period longer than their Eligibility Period (without regard to unapplied credits) or are otherwise not eligible Accounts, then all Accounts owing from that Account Debtor will be deemed ineligible for borrowing.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon may, from time to time, in its good faith business judgment, revise the Minimum Eligibility Requirements, upon written notice to Borrower.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Equipment</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means all present and future &ldquo;equipment&rdquo; as defined in the California Uniform Commercial Code in effect on the date hereof with such additions to such term as may hereafter be made, and includes without limitation all machinery, fixtures, goods, vehicles (including motor vehicles and trailers), and any interest in any of the foregoing.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">"</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Event of Default</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">" means any of the events set forth in Section&nbsp;7.1 of this Agreement.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">GAAP</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means generally accepted accounting principles consistently applied.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">General Intangibles</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means all present and future &ldquo;general intangibles&rdquo; as defined in the California Uniform Commercial Code in effect on the date hereof with such additions to such term as may hereafter be made, and includes without limitation all Intellectual Property, payment intangibles, royalties, contract rights, goodwill, franchise agreements, purchase orders, customer lists, route lists, telephone numbers, domain names, claims, income tax refunds, secu
rity and other deposits, options to purchase or sell real or personal property, rights in all litigation presently or hereafter pending (whether in contract, tort or otherwise), insurance policies (including without limitation key man, property damage, and business interruption insurance), payments of insurance and rights to payment of any kind.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">good faith business judgment</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">" means honesty in fact and good faith (as defined in Section 1201 of the Code) in the exercise of Silicon&rsquo;s business judgment.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">including</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means including (but not limited to).</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Intellectual Property</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means all present and future (a) copyrights, copyright rights, copyright applications, copyright registrations and like protections in each work of authorship and derivative work thereof, whether published or unpublished, (b) trade secret rights, including all rights to unpatented inventions and know</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&#8209;how, and confidential inf
ormation; (c) mask work or similar rights available for the protection of semiconductor chips; (d) patents, patent applications and like protections including without limitation improvements, divisions, continuations, renewals, reissues, extensions and continuations-in-part of the same; (e) trademarks, servicemarks, trade styles, and trade names, whether or not any of the foregoing are registered, and all applications to register and registrations of the same and like protections, and the entire goodwill of the business of Borrower connected with and symbolized by any such trademarks; (f) computer software and computer software products; (g) designs and design rights; (h) technology; (i) all claims for damages by way of past, present and future infringement of any of the rights included above; (j) all licenses or other rights to use any property or rights of a type described above.</em></em>

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Inventory</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means all present and future &ldquo;inventory&rdquo; as defined in the California Uniform Commercial Code in effect on the date hereof with such additions to such term as may hereafter be made, and includes without limitation&nbsp;&nbsp;all merchandise, raw materials, parts, supplies, packing and shipping materials, work in process and finished products, including without limitation such inventory as is temporarily out of Borrower&rsquo;s custody or possession 
or in transit and including any returned goods and any documents of title representing any of the above.</em></em>

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">"</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Material Adverse Change</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">" means any of the following: (i) a material adverse change in the business, operations, or financial or other condition of the Borrower, or (ii) a material impairment of the prospect of repayment of any portion of the Obligations; or (iii) a material impairment of the value or priority of Silicon&rsquo;s security interests in the Collateral.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">"</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Obligations</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">" means all present and future Loans, ad</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;vances, debts, liabilities, obligations, guaranties, covenants, duties and indebtedness at any time owing by Borrower to Silicon, whether evidenced by this Agreement or any note or other instrument or document, or otherwise, whether aris</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roma
n;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ing from an extension of credit, opening of a letter of credit, banker's acceptance, loan, guaranty, indemnifica</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion or otherwise, whether direct or indirect (including, without limitation, those acquired by assignment and any participation by Silicon in Borrower's debts owing to oth</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ers), absolute or contingent, due or to become due, includ</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ing, without limitation, all interest, charges, expenses, fees, attorney's fees, expert witness fees, audit fees, letter of credit fees, collateral monitoring fees, closing fees, facility fees, termination fees, minimum interest charges and any other sums chargeable to Borrower under t
his Agreement or under any other Loan Documents.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Other Property</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means the following as defined in the California Uniform Commercial Code in effect on the date hereof with such additions to such term as may hereafter be made, and all rights relating thereto: all present and future &ldquo;commercial tort claims&rdquo; (including without limitation any commercial tort claims identified in the Representations), &ldquo;documents&rdquo;, &ldquo;instruments&rdquo;, &ldquo;promissory notes&rdquo;, &ldquo;chattel paper&rdquo;, 
&ldquo;letters of credit&rdquo;, &ldquo;letter-of-credit rights&rdquo;, &ldquo;fixtures&rdquo;, &ldquo;farm products&rdquo; and &ldquo;money&rdquo;; and all other goods and personal property of every kind, tangible and intangible, whether or not governed by the California Uniform Commercial Code.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Payment</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means all checks, wire transfers and other items of payment received by Silicon (including proceeds of Accounts and payment of the Obligations in full) for credit to Borrower&rsquo;s outstanding Loans or, if the balance of the Loans have been reduced to zero, for credit to its Deposit Accounts.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">

m><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;housemen, carriers, or other similar liens arising in the or</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;dinary course of business and securing obligations which are not delinquent; (vii)&nbsp;liens incurred in connection with the extension, renewal or refinancing of the indebtedness secured by liens of the type described above in clauses (i) or (ii) above, provided that any extension, renewal or re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;placement lien is limited to the property encumbered by the existing lien and the principal amount of the indebted</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ness being extended, renewed or refinanced does not in</em><em style="font-styl
e:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;crease; (viii) Liens in favor of customs and revenue author</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ities which secure payment of customs duties in connec</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion with the importation of goods.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon will have the right to require, as a condition to its consent under sub</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;paragraph (iv) above, that the holder of the additional se</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;curity interest or lien sign an intercreditor agreement on Silicon&rsquo;s then standard form, acknowledge that the secu</em><em style="font-style:normal;fo
nt-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;rity interest is subordinate to the security interest in favor of Silicon, and agree not to take any action to enforce its subordinate security interest so long as any Obligations remain outstanding, and that Borrower agree that any un</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;cured default in any obligation secured by the subordinate security interest shall also constitute an Event of Default under this Agreement.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">"</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Person</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">" means any individual, sole proprietorship, partnership, joint venture, trust, unincorporated organiza</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion, association, corporation, government, or any agency or political division thereof, or any other entity. .</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&ldquo;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Representations</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&rdquo; means the written Representations and Warranties provided by Borrower to Silicon referred to in the Schedule.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">"</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Reserves</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">" means, as of any date of determination, such amounts as Silicon may from time to time establish and revise in its good faith business judgment, reducing the amount of Loans, Letters of Credit and other financial accommodations which would otherwise be available to Borrower under the lending formula(s) provided in the Schedule:&nbsp;&nbsp;(a) to reflect events, conditions, contingencies or risks which, as determined by Silicon in its good faith business judgment, do or may a
dversely affect (i) the Collateral or any other property which is security for the Obligations or its value (including without limitation any increase in delinquencies of Accounts), (ii) the assets, business or prospects of Borrower or any Guarantor, or (iii) the security interests and other rights of Silicon in the Collateral (including the enforceability, perfection and priority thereof); or (b) to reflect Silicon's good faith belief that any collateral report or financial information furnished by or on behalf of Borrower or any Guarantor to Silicon is or may have been incomplete, inaccurate or misleading in any material respect; or (c) in respect of any state of facts which Silicon determines in good faith constitutes an Event of Default or may, with notice or passage of time or both, constitute an Event of Default.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;">9.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">GENERAL PROVISIONS.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:13.5pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">9.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Interest Computation; Float Charge.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;In computing interest on the Obligations, all Payments received after 12:00 Noon on any day shall be deemed received on the next Business Day.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, Silicon shall be entitled to charge Borrower a &ldquo;float&rdquo; charge in an amount equal to two Business Days interest, at the interest rate applicable to the Loans, on all Payments received by Silicon. Said float charge is not included in interest for purposes of computing Minimum Monthly Interest (if any) under this Agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;The float charge for eac
h month shall be payable on the last day of the month.&nbsp;&nbsp;Bank shall not be required to credit Borrower's account for the amount of any item of payment which is unsatisfactory to Bank in its good faith business judgment, and Bank may charge Borrower's loan account for the amount of any item of payment which is returned to Bank unpaid.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">9.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Application of Payments.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">All payments with re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;spect to the Obligations shall be applied to the Obligations, in such order and manner as Silicon shall determine in its good faith business judgment.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">9.3&nbsp;&nbsp;Charges to Accounts.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">Silicon may, in its discretion, require that Borrower pay monetary Obligations in cash to Silicon, or charge them to Borrower&rsquo;s Loan account, in which event they will bear interest at the same rate appli</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;cable to the Loans.&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon may also, in its discretion, charge any monetary Obligations to Borrower&rsquo;s Deposit Accounts maintained with Silicon.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">9.4&nbsp;&nbsp;Monthly Accountings.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon shall provide Borrower monthly with an account of advances, charges, expenses and payments made pursuant to this Agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;Such account shall be deemed correct, accurate and bind</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ing on Borrower and an account stated (except for reverses and reapplications of payments made and corrections of er</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;
rors discovered by Silicon), unless Borrower notifies Silicon in writing to the contrary within 60 days after such account is rendered, describing the nature of any al</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;leged errors or omissions.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">9.5&nbsp;&nbsp;Notices.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;All notices to be given under this Agreement shall be in writing and shall be given either personally or by reputable private delivery service or by regular first-class mail, or certified mail return receipt re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;quested, addressed to Silicon or Borrower at the addresses shown in the heading to this Agreement, or at any other address designated in writing by one party to the other party.&nbsp;&nbsp;Notices to Silicon shall be directed to the Co
mmercial Finance Division, to the attention of the Division Manager or the Division Credit Manager.&nbsp;&nbsp;All no</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tices shall be deemed to have been given upon delivery in the case of notices personally delivered, or at the expira</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tion of one Business Day following delivery to the private delivery service, or two Business Days following the de</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;posit thereof in the </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">United States</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;mail, with postage pre</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Pala
tino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;paid.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">9.6&nbsp;&nbsp;Severability.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Should any provision of this Agreement be held by any court of competent jurisdiction to be void or unenforceable, such defect shall not affect the remainder of this Agreement, which shall continue in full force and effect.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">

de all prior and contemporaneous negotiations and oral representations and agreements, all of which are merged and integrated in this Agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">There are no oral under</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">&shy;standings, representations or agreements between the par</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none underline;">&shy;ties which are not set forth in this Agreement or in other written agreements signed by the parties in connection herewith.</em></em>
