<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Palatino;font-size:12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;text-indent:72pt;text-indent:9pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">9.8&nbsp;&nbsp;Waivers; Indemnity.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;The failure of Silicon at any time or times to require Borrower to strictly comply with any of the pro</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;visions of this Agreement or any other Loan Document shall not waive or diminish any right of Silicon later to demand and re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ceive strict compliance therewith.&nbsp;&nbsp;Any waiver of any de</em><em style="font-st
yle:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;fault shall not waive or affect any other default, whether prior or subsequent, and whether or not similar.&nbsp;&nbsp;None of the provisions of this Agreement or any other Loan Document shall be deemed to have been waived by any act or knowledge of Silicon or its agents or employees, but only by a specific written waiver signed by an authorized officer of Silicon and delivered to Borrower.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower waives the benefit of all statutes of limitations relating to any of the Obligations or this Agreement or any other Loan Document, and Borrower waives demand, protest, notice of protest and notice of de</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;fault or dishonor, notice of payment and nonpayment, re</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;lease, compromise,
 settlement, extension or renewal of any commercial paper, instrument, account, General Intangible, document or guaranty at any time held by Silicon on which Borrower is or may in any way be liable, and notice of any action taken by Silicon, unless expressly required by this Agreement. Borrower hereby agrees to indemnify Silicon and its affiliates, subsidiaries, parent, directors, officers, employees, agents, and attorneys, and to hold them harmless from and against any and all claims, debts, liabilities, demands, obligations, actions, causes of action, penalties, costs and expenses (including reasonable attor</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;neys' fees), of every kind, which they may sustain or incur based upon or arising out of any of the Obligations, or any relationship or agreement between Silicon and Borrower, or any other matter, relating to Borrower or the Obligations; provided that this indemnity shall&nbsp;&nbsp;not
 extend to damages proximately caused by the indemnitee&rsquo;s own gross negligence or willful misconduct.&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding any provision in this Agreement to the contrary, the indemnity agreement set forth in this Section shall survive any termination of this Agreement and shall for all purposes continue in full force and effect.</em></em>

rson affiliated with or representing Silicon, but nothing herein shall relieve Silicon from liability for its own gross negligence or willful misconduct.</em></em>

limited to, any reasonable attorneys' fees and costs Silicon incurs in order to do the following: prepare and negotiate this Agreement and all present and future documents relating to this Agreement; obtain legal advice in connection with this Agreement or Borrower; en</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;force, or seek to enforce, any of its rights; prosecute ac</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;tions against, or defend actions by, Account Debtors; commence, intervene in, or defend any action or proceed</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&shy;ing; initiate any complaint to be relieved of the automatic stay in bankruptcy; file or prosecute any probate claim, bankruptcy claim, third-party claim, or other claim; exam</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Palatino;f

irectors, officers, employees, agents, accountants or attorneys, shall be barred unless asserted by Borrower by the commencement of an action or proceeding in a court of competent jurisdiction by the filing of a complaint within one year after the first act, occurrence or omission upon which such claim or cause of action, or any part thereof, is based, and the service of a summons and complaint on an officer of Silicon, or on any other person authorized to accept service on behalf of Silicon, within thirty (30) days thereafter.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower agrees that such one-year period is a reasonable and sufficient time for Borrower to investigate and act upon any such claim or cause of action.&nbsp;&nbsp;The one-year period provided herein shall not be waived, tolled, or extended except by the written consent of Silicon in its sole discretion.&nbsp;&nbsp;This provision shall survive any termination of this Loan Agreement or any other Loan Document.</em></em>

certainty or ambiguity in any term or provision of this Agreement shall be construed strictly against Silicon or Borrower under any rule of construction or otherwise.</em></em>

ormal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">the sum or (a) and (b) below:</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;margin-left:198pt;text-indent:0pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">(a)</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">85% </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">(an &ldquo;Advance Rate&rdquo;) of the amount of Borrower&rsquo;s Eligible Accounts (as defined in Section 8 above), plus</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;margin-left:198pt;text-indent:0pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;an amount not to exceed the least of:&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;margin-left:234pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">(1)<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">50% </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">(an &ldquo;Advance Rate&rdquo;) of the value of Borrower's Eligible Inventory (as defined in Section 8 above), calculated at the lower of cost or market value and determined on a first-in, first-out basis, or</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;margin-left:234pt;text-indent:-18pt;">

</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:234pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-left:234pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">

</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:Tms Rmn;margin-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-126pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:none underline;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:none underline;">Services and Reserves</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">:&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower may utilize up to $10,000 of Silicon&rsquo;s Cash Management Services (as defined below), consisting of business credit card services, as identified in the cash management services agreement related to the same (the &ldquo;Cash Management Services&rdquo;).&nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon may, in its sole discretion, reserve against Loans which would otherwise be available hereunder such sums up to $5
,000 as Silicon shall determine in its good faith business judgment in connection with the Cash Management Services, and Silicon may charge to Borrower&rsquo;s Loan account or deposit accounts, any amounts that may become due or owing to Silicon in connection with the Cash Management Services.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower agrees to execute and deliver to Silicon all standard form applications and agreements of Silicon in connection with the Cash Management Services, and, without limiting any of the terms of such applications and agreements, Borrower will pay all standard fees and charges of Silicon in connection with the Cash Management Services.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Cash Management Services shall terminate on the Maturity Date.</em></em>

pt;">6.5%</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;per annum.&nbsp;&nbsp;Interest shall be calculated on the basis of a 360-day year for the actual number of days elapsed.&nbsp;&nbsp;As used in this Agreement, "Prime Rate" means the interest rate announced from time to time by Silicon as its &ldquo;prime rate&rdquo; (which is a base rate upon which other rates charged by Silicon are based, and it is not necessarily the best rate available at Silicon).&nbsp;&nbsp;The interest rate applicable to the Obligations shall change on each date there is a change in the Prime Rate.</em></em>

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Loan Fee:</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">$45,000</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">, payable concurrently herewith, plus $45,000 on the first anniversary of the date of this Agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;$6,250 of the fee previously paid by Borrower to Silicon shall be credited against the portion of this fee payable on the date hereof.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">

</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(Section 5.1):</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower shall comply with each of the following covenants.&nbsp;&nbsp;Compliance shall be determined as of the end of each month, except as otherwise specifically provided below: </em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Minimum Tangible </em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Net Worth:</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Borrower shall maintain a Tangible Net Worth of not less than $775,000 plus (i) 50% of any increase in Tangible Net Worth arising from any forgiveness of indebtedness of Borrower, plus (ii) 50% of all consideration received after the date hereof for equity securities and subordinated debt of the Borrower, plus (iii) 50% of the Borrower&rsquo;s net i
ncome in each fiscal quarter ending after the date hereof.&nbsp;&nbsp;Increases in the Minimum Tangible Net Worth Covenant based on forgiveness of indebtedness shall be effective as of the end of the month in which such forgiveness occurs, and shall continue effective thereafter. Increases in the Minimum Tangible Net Worth Covenant based on consideration received for equity securities and subordinated debt of the Borrower shall be effective as of the end of the month in which such consideration is received, and shall continue effective thereafter.&nbsp;&nbsp;Increases in the Minimum Tangible Net Worth Covenant based on net income shall be effective on the last day of the fiscal quarter in which said net income is realized, and shall continue effective thereafter. In no event shall the Minimum Tangible Net Worth Covenant be decreased. </em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Definitions.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">For purposes of the foregoing financial covenants, the following term shall have the following meaning:</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&ldquo;Tangible Net Worth&rdquo; shall mean the excess of total assets less total liabilities, determined in accordance with GAAP, with the following adjustments:&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-162pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-180pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(A) there shall be excluded from assets:&nbsp;&nbsp;(i) notes, accounts receivable and other obligations owing to Borrower from its officers or other Affiliates, and (ii) all assets which would be classified as intangible assets under GAAP, including without limitation goodwill, licenses, patents, trademarks, trade names, copyrights, ca
pitalized software and organizational costs, licenses and franchises, and (iii) minority investments in other Persons.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-180pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(B) there shall be excluded from liabilities:&nbsp;&nbsp;all indebtedness which is subordinated to the Obligations under a subordination agreement in form specified by Silicon or by language in the instrument evidencing the indebtedness which Silicon agrees in writing is acceptable to Silicon in its good faith business judgment.</em></e
m>
</p>

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>

<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-transform:uppercase;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Reporting.</em></em>

</em></td>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-right:1pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(Section 5.3):</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Borrower shall provide Silicon with the following:</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">1.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Transaction reports and schedules of collections, each week and at the time of each Loan request, on Silicon's standard form</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">2.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Monthly accounts receivable agings, aged by invoice date, within fifteen days after the end of each month.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">3.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Monthly accounts payable agings, aged by invoice date, and outstanding or held check registers, if any, within fifteen days after the end of each month. </em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">4.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Monthly reconciliations of accounts receivable agings (aged by invoice date), transaction reports, and general ledger, within fifteen days after the end of each month. </em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">5.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Monthly perpetual inventory reports for the Inventory valued on a first-in, first-out basis at the lower of cost or market (in accordance with GAAP) or such other inventory reports as are requested by Silicon in its good faith business judgment, all within fifteen days after the end of each month. </em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">6.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Monthly unaudited financial statements, as soon as available, and in any event within thirty days after the end of each month. </em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">7.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Monthly Compliance Certificates, within thirty days after the end of each month, in such form as Silicon shall reasonably specify, signed by the Chief Financial Officer of Borrower, certifying that as of the end of such month Borrower was in full compliance with all of the terms and conditions of this Agreement, and setting forth calculations showing compliance with the financial covenants set forth in this Agreement and such other information as Silicon shall reasonably request, including, without limitati
on, a statement that at the end of such month there were no held checks.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">8.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Copies of Borrower&rsquo;s Reports to the Securities Exchange Commission on Forms 10-Q and 10-K within three days after the earlier of the date they are filed or are required to be filed with the Securities Exchange Commission.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">9.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Annual operating budgets (including income statements, balance sheets and cash flow statements, by month) for the upcoming fiscal year of Borrower within thirty days prior to the end of each fiscal year of Borrower.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:162pt;text-indent:-18pt;margin-bottom:8pt;margin-left:180pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-18pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">10.<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Annual financial statements, as soon as available, and in any event within 90 days following the end of Borrower's fiscal year, certified by, and with an unqualified opinion of, independent certified public accountants acceptable to Silicon.</em></em>
</p>

.</em></em>

</em></td>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189.35pt;margin-right:0.7pt;text-indent:-27.35pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Banking Relationship.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Borrower shall at all times maintain its primary banking relationship with Silicon. Without limiting the generality of the foregoing, Borrower shall, at all times, maintain not less than 100% of its total cash and investments on deposit with Silicon. </em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">(2)</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Subordination of Inside Debt</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;All present and future indebtedness of Borrower to its officers, directors and shareholders (excluding salaries, bonuses, options, including options for cash with equity, fees for services and other amounts due by Borrower in the nature of compensation) (&ldquo;Inside Debt&rdquo;) shall, at all times, be subor
dinated to the Obligations pursuant to a subordination agreement on Silicon&rsquo;s standard form.&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower represents and warrants that there is no Inside Debt presently outstanding.&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to incurring any Inside Debt in the future, Borrower shall cause the person to whom such Inside Debt will be owed to execute and deliver to Silicon a subordination agreement on Silicon&rsquo;s standard form.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">(3)</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Qualification. </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;Within 45 days after the date hereof, M-Wave, Inc. shall qualify to do business in the State of </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Illinois</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;and shall provide evidence of the same to Silicon which is reasonably satisfactory to Silicon.</em></em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em>&nbsp;</em>
</p>
<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">(4)</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><a name="OLE_LINK179"></a><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Warrants.</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower is concurrently executing and delivering to Silicon a seven-year warrant to purchase shares of common stock of the Borrower, at the price and on the terms therein set forth.&nbsp;&nbsp;Said warrant shall replace the Warrant dated March 31, 2004 previously issued to Silicon.&nbsp;&nbsp;Said warrants shall be deemed fully earned on the date hereof, shall be in addition to
 all interest and other fees, and shall be non-refundable.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;text-indent:-27pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">(5)<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Use of Proceeds; Past-Due Payables.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Borrower shall not use more than $200,000 of proceeds of Loans for the payment of trade payables of Borrower which are in existence at the date hereof and are aged more than 120 days from their due date (the &ldquo;Past-Due Payables&rdquo;).&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower anticipates selling its real property located at 215 Park, </em><em style=
"font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Bensenville</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">, </em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Illinois</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;(the &ldquo;Real Property&rdquo;), and Borrower anticipates receiving a tax refund in the amount of approximately $730,000 (the &ldquo;Tax Refund&rdquo;).&nbsp;&nbsp;Borrower shall use the proceeds of such sale and tax refund to pay in full the Past-Due Payables, and any excess may be retained by Borrower for use in its business.</em></em>

<p style="margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;font-size:10pt;margin-left:189pt;text-indent:-27pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;margin-left:189pt;margin-right:1pt;text-indent:-27pt;">
<em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Tms Rmn;"><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;background:transparent;font-family:Times New Roman;">(6)<em style="font-size:7pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-decoration:none;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman"> </em></em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Subsidiary.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em><em style="font-style:normal;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;">Borrower represents, warrants and covenants that (i) it has no subsidiaries except for Poly Circuits, Inc., an Illinois corporation (the &ldquo;Sub&rdquo;), (ii) the Sub shall be merged with and into Borrower in a merger in which the Borrower is the surviving corporation, within 60 days after the date hereof, and Borrower shall provide writt
en evidence of the same to Silicon with said 60-day period, and (iii) the Sub is, and, until such merger is consummated, will continue to be, a shell corporation with no assets or business.</em></em>
